% Spin
\newpage
\section{Spin and \(L\)}
\subsection{Hydrogen Atom}

% L_z and L^2 and L_{+-}
\noindent
\(
    \begin{aligned}[t]
        & \text{\underline{Angular Momentum}}:
            \\[5pt]
        & \boxed{ \widehat{L_i} \equiv ( \vec{r} \times \vec{p} )_i }
            \hspace{5pt}, \hspace{5pt} \boxed{ L_z = \tfrac{\hbar}{i} \tfrac{\partial}{\partial \phi}}
            \\
        & \boxed{ \widehat{L}_{\pm} \equiv \widehat{L}_x \pm i \widehat{L}_y } \\
        & \boxed{ \widehat{L}^2 \equiv L_x^2 + L_y^2 + L_z^2 } \\
        & \boxed{ L_\pm L_\mp = \widehat{L}^2 - L_z^2 \pm \hbar L_z  }
    \end{aligned}
\)
\hfill
% Commutation Relations
\begin{minipage}[t]{.6\textwidth}
    \underline{Commutation Relations}:

    % [ L_x , L_y ]
    \vspace{10pt} \noindent \(
        \boxed{ \big[ \hat{x} , L_y \big] = i \hbar \hat{z} } 
        \ , \
        \boxed{ \big[ p_x , L_y \big] = i \hbar p_z }
        \ , \ 
        \boxed{ \big[ L_x , L_y \big] = i \hbar L_z } 
    \) %\ \ {\scriptsize (can't measure concurrently)}

    % [ H , _ ]
    \vspace{10pt} \noindent \(
        \boxed{ \big[ L^2 , L_i \big] = \big[ H , L_i \big] = \big[ H , L^2 \big] = 0}
    \) \ \ {\scriptsize (can measure concurrently)}

    % [ L^2 , L_z ]
    \vspace{10pt} \noindent \( 
        \rightarrow \ 
        \begin{aligned}
            \Aboxed{ L_z Y_{m'} & = \hbar m' Y_{m'} }\\[5pt]
            \Aboxed{ L^2 Y_{m'} & = \hbar^2 \lambda_{m'} Y_{m'} }
        \end{aligned}
        \ \Rightarrow \ 
        \begin{aligned}
            & \langle L^2 - L_z^2 \rangle 
                = \langle L_x^2 + L_y^2 \rangle 
                \geq 0
                \\[5pt]
            & \bullet \ \sqrt{\lambda_{m'}} 
                \geq \ m' \geq -\sqrt{\lambda_{m'}}
        \end{aligned} 
    \)
\end{minipage}

% [ __ , L_{+-} ]
\vspace{20pt} \noindent
\textbf{Let} \ \( (L_\pm)^n Y_\mu \equiv | m \rangle \) \hspace{10pt} {\scriptsize(see harm. osc. for why ladders)}\\[10pt]
\hspace{18pt} 
\begin{tabular}{c c l}
    \(
        \boxed{ \big[ \tfrac{L_z}{\hbar} , L_\pm \big] = (\pm 1) L_\pm }
        \hspace{10pt} \Rightarrow \hspace{10pt}
        \big[ \tfrac{L_z}{\hbar} , (L_\pm)^n \big] = \pm n (L_\pm)^n
        \)
        & \( \ \Rightarrow \ \) 
        & \( \begin{aligned}
                L_z \big[ (L_\pm)^n Y_\mu \big] &= (\mu \pm n )\hbar \big[ (L_\pm)^n Y_\mu \big]\\[5pt]
                \bullet \ L_z | m \rangle 
                    &= (\mu \pm n )\hbar | m \rangle
            \end{aligned} \) 
        \\[.8cm] 
    \( 
        \boxed{ \big[ L^2 , L_\pm \big] = 0 } 
        \hspace{10pt} \Rightarrow \hspace{10pt}
        \big[ L^2 , (L_\pm)^n \big] = 0 
        \)
        & \( \ \Rightarrow \ \)
        & \( \begin{aligned}
            L^2 \big[ (L_\pm)^n Y_\mu \big] &= \lambda_\mu \big[ (L_\pm)^n Y_\mu \big] \\[5pt]
            \bullet \ L^2 | m \rangle
                &= \lambda_\mu | m \rangle
        \end{aligned} \)
\end{tabular}

% Solve for Eigenvalues and Eigenfunctions
\vspace{25pt} \noindent 
\textbf{Then} \ \( 
    \Big( \sqrt{\lambda_\mu} \ \geq \ (\mu \pm n) \ \geq \ -\sqrt{\lambda_\mu} \ \Big)
    \ \Rightarrow 
\) \ \textbf{Let} \ \ \ {\scriptsize (else un-normalizable solution)}

\vspace{10pt}\noindent
\(
    \hfill
    \begin{aligned}
        & \underline{ L_+ | m_t \rangle = 0 } \ , \ \ L_z | m_t \rangle = \hbar l \ , \\[5pt]
        & L^2 | m_t \rangle = \lambda \hbar^2 \ , \ \ L^2 = L_- L_+ + L_z^2 + \hbar L_z \\[10pt]
        & \bullet \ L^2 | m_t \rangle = \hbar^2 l (l+1) | m_t \rangle = \lambda \hbar^2 | m_t \rangle
    \end{aligned}
    \hfill\vline\hfill
    \begin{aligned}
        & \underline{ L_- | m_b \rangle = 0 } \ , \ \ L_z | m_b \rangle = \hbar l' \ , \\[5pt]
        & L^2 | m_b \rangle = \lambda \hbar^2 \ , \ \ L^2 = L_+ L_- + L_z^2 - \hbar L_z \\[10pt]
        & \bullet \ L^2 | m_b \rangle = \hbar^2 l' (l'-1) | m_b \rangle = \lambda \hbar^2 | m_b \rangle    
    \end{aligned}
    \hfill\hs
\)

\vspace{10pt} \noindent
\hfill
\( 
    \Big[ \lambda = l' (l'-1) = l (l+1) \Big]
    \ \Rightarrow \ 
    \big[ l' = -l \big]
    \ \Rightarrow \ 
    \left[ \begin{aligned}
        L_z | m_t \rangle &= \hbar l \hs | m_t \rangle \\
        L_z | m_b \rangle &= - \hbar l \hs | m_b \rangle
    \end{aligned} \right]
\) \ \ \parbox{3.3cm}{\scriptsize (Spherical Harmonics do not allow half-integer \(l\))} 
\hfill\hs

% Solutions
\vspace{15pt} \noindent 
Schrodinger \(Y_l^m\): \ \fbox{ 
    \( \begin{gathered}
        l \in \left\{ 0 , 1 , 2, ... \right\} \\[5pt]
        m \in \{ -l , -l + 1, ... , l-1 , l \}
    \end{gathered} \)
    \hspace{.2cm}
    \rule[-25pt]{.5pt}{55pt}
    \hspace{.2cm}
    \( \begin{aligned}
        L_z \big| Y_l^m \big\rangle & = \hbar m \big| Y_l^m \big\rangle 
            = \tfrac{\hbar}{i} \tfrac{\partial}{\partial \phi} \big| Y_l^m \big\rangle 
            \\[5pt]
        L^2 \big| Y_l^m \big\rangle & = \hbar^2 l (l+1) \big| Y_l^m \big\rangle \\[5pt]
        L_\pm \big| Y_l^m \big\rangle & =
            \hbar \sqrt{\scriptstyle l(l+1) - m(m \pm 1)} \ \big| Y_l^m  \big\rangle
    \end{aligned} \)     
} 

%---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
%
%
%---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
\newpage \noindent
% Generalized Angular Momentum
\subsection{Generalized}
\noindent
\(
    % Angular Momentum
    \begin{aligned}[t]
        & \text{\underline{Angular Momentum}:}
            \\[5pt]
        & \begin{array}[t]{l l}
                \widehat{J}_i \equiv \text{???} & \boxed{ J^2 \equiv J_x^2 + J_y^2 + J_z^2 } \\[10pt]
                \boxed{ J_\pm \equiv J_x \pm i J_y } & \boxed{ J_\pm J_\mp = J^2 - J_z^2 \pm \hbar J_z }
            \end{array}
    \end{aligned}
    \hfill
    % Commutation Relations
    \begin{aligned}[t]
        & \text{\underline{Commutation Relations}:} \\[5pt]
        % [ J_x , J_y ]
        & \boxed{ \big[ J_i , J_j \big] = i \hbar J_k \ \epsilon_{ij} }
            \ \Leftrightarrow\ 
            \boxed{ J \times J = i \hbar J }
            \\[10pt]
        % [ J^2 , J_z ]
        & \boxed{ \big[ J^2 , J_z \big] = 0 } = \big[ H , J_z \big]
            \hspace{10pt} \text{\scriptsize (if spher. symm.)}
    \end{aligned}
    \hfill\hs
\)

% General Eigenvalues
\vspace{15pt} \noindent
General: \ \fbox{ 
    \( 
        \begin{gathered}
            j \in \left\{ 0 , \tfrac{1}{2}, 1 , \tfrac{3}{2}, ... \right\} \\[5pt]
            m \in \{ -j , -j + 1, ... , j-1 , j \}
        \end{gathered}
        \hspace{10pt}\vline\hspace{10pt}
        \begin{aligned}
            J_z \big| j m \big\rangle & = \hbar m \big| j m \big\rangle \\[5pt]
            J^2 \big| j m \big\rangle & = \hbar^2 j (j+1) \big| j m \big\rangle \\[5pt]
            J_\pm \big| j m \big\rangle & =
                \hbar \sqrt{\scriptstyle j(j+1) - m(m \pm 1)} \ \big| j m  \big\rangle
                \\[5pt]
            J_x \big| j m \big\rangle & = \tfrac{ J_{+} + J_{-} }{2} \big| j m \big\rangle
        \end{aligned} 
    \)     
}

\vspace{15pt}\noindent
% Generator of Rotations
\text{\underline{Generator of Rotations}:}\\[10pt]
\(\displaystyle
    U [R \mss{(\theta)}] = e^{- \tfrac{i}{\hbar} \theta \hs \hat{\theta} \cdot L} 
    = \lim_{N \rightarrow \infty} \left[ \mathbbm{1} - \tfrac{i}{\hbar} \tfrac{\theta}{N} \hs \hat{\theta} \cdot L \right]^N
    \ \Leftrightarrow\ \boxed{ U[R\mss{(\epsilon_z \hs \hat{z})}] = \mathbbm{1} - \tfrac{i}{\hbar} \epsilon_z L_z }
\)

\vspace{15pt}\noindent
\(
    1.)\ \ \begin{aligned}[t]
        & U[R\mss{(\epsilon_z \hat{z})}] \mss{|x,y \rangle} \equiv \mss{|x - \epsilon_z y , \hs \epsilon_z x + y \rangle}\\
        & \Rightarrow\ \langle \mss{x,y} | U[R\mss{(\epsilon_z \hat{z})}] | \Psi \rangle
            = \Psi \mss{(x + \epsilon_z y , \hs \epsilon_z x - y)}
            \\
        & \Rightarrow\ \underline{ \langle \mss{x,y} | L_z | \Psi \rangle = (XP_y - YP_x) \Psi \mss{(x,y)} }
    \end{aligned}
    \hfill
    % Commutators
    \text{or\ \ } 2.)\ \ \begin{aligned}[t]
        & \begin{aligned}[t]
                U^\dagger X U \equiv X - \epsilon_z Y & \ \Rightarrow\ [X, L_z] = - i\hbar Y \\
                U^\dagger P_y U \equiv \epsilon_z P_x + P_y & \ \Rightarrow\ [P_y, L_z] = i\hbar P_x \\
                \mss{ U^\dagger Y U,\ U^\dagger P_x U, } & \ \Rightarrow\ \dots
            \end{aligned}
            \\[5pt]
        & \Rightarrow\ \underline{L_z = XP_y - YP_x}
    \end{aligned}
\)

\vspace{10pt}\noindent
% Consistency Check
\textit{Consistency Check}:\ \
\(
    \begin{aligned}[t]
        & U[\mss{ R(- \epsilon_z \hat{z}) }] \hs T \mss{ (- \epsilon_x \hat{x} - \epsilon_y \hat{y}) }
            \hs U[\mss{ R(\epsilon_z \hat{z}) }] \hs T \mss{ (\epsilon_x \hat{x} + \epsilon_y \hat{y}) }
            = T \mss{( - \epsilon_y \epsilon_z \hat{x} + \epsilon_x \epsilon_z \hat{y} )}
            \\
        & ? U[\mss{ R(- \epsilon_y \hat{y}) }] U[\mss{ R(- \epsilon_x \hat{x}) }] 
            U[\mss{ R(\epsilon_y \hat{y}) }] U[\mss{ R(\epsilon_x \hat{x}) }] 
            = \begin{gathered}[t]
                \mathbbm{1} + \tfrac{i}{\hbar} \epsilon_x \epsilon_y L_z \\
                \mss{(L_z = x p_y - y p_x)}
            \end{gathered}
            = U [\mss{ R(-\epsilon_x \epsilon_y \hat{z}) }] 
    \end{aligned}
\)

\vspace{5pt}\noindent
% Tensors and Tensor Operators
\underline{Tensors and Tensor Operators}

\vspace{10pt}\noindent
\(
    \hfill
    \begin{aligned}[t]
        & \textit{rank-2 Tensor}: \\
        & \hspace{10pt} \begin{aligned}
                | t^{(2)} \rangle & = \mss{ \sum_{i=1}^{3} \sum_{j=1}^{3} }\ t_{ij} \hs | i \rangle | j \rangle \\[5pt]
                & = \mss{ \sum_{i=1}^{3} \sum_{j=1}^{3} }\ | i j \rangle \langle i j | t^{(2)} \rangle
            \end{aligned}
            \\[10pt]
        & \textit{rank-\(2\) Cartesian Tens. Oper.,}\ T_{ij}: \\
        & \hspace{10pt} \mss{ \text{Set of } 3^{n=2} \text{ Operators}}\\[5pt]
    \end{aligned}
    \hfill\vline\hfill
    \begin{aligned}[t]
        & \textit{rank-\(k\) Spherical Tensor Operator,}\ T^q_k: \\
        & \hspace{10pt} \mss{ \text{Set of } 2k+1 \text{ Operators \ s.t. } }\\
        & \hspace{10pt} \begin{aligned}[t]
                U[R] \hs T^q_k \hs U^\dagger [R] & = \mss{ \sum^k_{q'=-k} D^{k}_{q'q} \hs T^{q'}_k } \\[-5pt]
                & \hs \downarrow\\
                U T^q_k U^\dagger U | j m \rangle & = 
                    \mss{ \displaystyle \sum_{q'} \sum_{m'} D^k_{q'q} D^j_{m'm} \hs T^k_{q'} | j m' \rangle }
                    \\[5pt]
                \sim\ U |k q \rangle | j m \rangle & = 
                    \mss{ \displaystyle \sum_{q'} \sum_{m'} D^k_{q'q} D^j_{m'm} | k q' \rangle | j m' \rangle }
            \end{aligned}
            \hspace{10pt}
            \bullet\ \arraycolsep=2pt \begin{array}[t]{l c l}
                T_1^{\pm1} & = 
                    & \mp \tfrac{V_x \pm i V_y}{\sqrt{2}}
                    \\[5pt]
                T_1^0 & = 
                    & V_z
            \end{array}
    \end{aligned}
    \hfill\hs
\)

\vspace{15pt}\noindent
% Wigner-Eckhart Theorem
\(
    \textit{Wigner-Eckhart}:\ \ 
    \langle \alpha_2 j_2 m_2 | \hs T_k^q \hs | \alpha_1 j_1 m_1 \rangle
    = \langle \alpha_2 j_2 |\hs T_k \hs | \alpha_1 j_1 \rangle 
    \cdot \begin{gathered}[t]
        \langle j_2 m_2 | kq ; j_1 m_1 \rangle\\[-3pt]
        \text{\scriptsize(CG coeff.)}
    \end{gathered}
\)

\vfill

%-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
%
%
%-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
% Spin 1/2
\newpage
\subsection{1 Particle w/ Spin, \ \(s = \frac{1}{2}\)}
*Find the Eigenvectors, \(e_i\) , of \(S_z\) and \(S^2\) in the form of \(
    |\chi\rangle = 
    \mss{ \left(\begin{matrix}
        \cos\tfrac{\theta}{2} \hs e^{i\phi_1} \\[3pt]
        \sin\tfrac{\theta}{2} \hs e^{i\phi_2}
    \end{matrix}\right) }
    =
    \mss{ e^{i\gamma} \left(\begin{matrix}
        \cos\tfrac{\theta}{2} \hs e^{-i \frac{\phi}{2}} \\[3pt]
        \sin\tfrac{\theta}{2} \hs e^{i \frac{\phi}{2}}
    \end{matrix}\right) }
    \hfill
    \mss{ \begin{aligned}
        & \gamma = \tfrac{\phi_1 + \phi_2}{2}\\
        & \phi = \phi_2 - \phi_1
    \end{aligned} }
\)

% States
\begin{center}
    * \fbox{ 
        \( 
            e_i \in \left\{ \ \ 
                | \tfrac{1}{2} \ \tfrac{1}{2} \rangle 
                \equiv | \uparrow \ \rangle \equiv 
                \left( \begin{matrix} 
                    1 \\
                    0
                \end{matrix} \right)
                = \tfrac{1}{2} (1 + \sigma_z)
                \hspace{.5cm} , \hspace{.5cm}
                | \tfrac{1}{2} \ \tfrac{-1}{2}  \rangle 
                \equiv | \downarrow \ \rangle \equiv 
                \left( \begin{matrix} 
                    0 \\
                    1
                \end{matrix} \right)
                = \tfrac{\sigma_x}{2} (1 + \sigma_z)
                \ \ \right\} 
        \) 
    }
\end{center}

\vspace{5pt} \noindent
\(\begin{array}{c c l}
    % S^2
    \left. \begin{aligned}
            S^2 | \uparrow \ \rangle = \tfrac{3\hbar^2}{4} | \uparrow \ \rangle \\[10pt]
            S^2 | \downarrow \ \rangle = \tfrac{3\hbar^2}{4} | \downarrow \ \rangle
        \end{aligned} \hspace{18pt} \right\}
        & \Rightarrow
        & \begin{aligned}
                & S^2 = \frac{3\hbar^2}{4}
                    \left( \begin{matrix} 
                        1 & 0 \\
                        0 & 1
                    \end{matrix} \right) 
                    = \frac{3\hbar^2}{4} \sigma_0
                    = * \left( \begin{matrix} 
                        1 & 0 \\
                        0 & 1
                    \end{matrix} \right) 
                    \left( \begin{matrix} 
                        \tfrac{3\hbar^2}{4} & 0 \\
                        0 & \tfrac{3\hbar^2}{4}
                    \end{matrix} \right) 
                    \left( \begin{matrix} 
                        1 & 0 \\
                        0 & 1
                    \end{matrix} \right)^{T*}
                    \\
                & = \text{\scriptsize \underline{Casimir Op}: \( - (g_{yz})^2 - (g_{zx})^2 - (g_{xy})^2 \)}
                    = \tfrac{3 \hbar^2}{4} \mathbbm{1}
                    \hspace{20pt} (\text{\scriptsize only for \(s=1/2\) systems})
            \end{aligned}
        \\[35pt]
    % S_+-
    \left. \begin{gathered}
            S_- | \uparrow \ \rangle = \hbar | \downarrow \ \rangle \\[10pt]
            S_+ | \downarrow \ \rangle = \hbar | \uparrow \ \rangle \\[10pt]
            S_+ | \uparrow \ \rangle = S_- | \downarrow \ \rangle = 0
        \end{gathered} \hspace{18pt} \right\}
        & \Rightarrow
        & \begin{aligned}
                S_+ & = \hbar
                    \left( \begin{matrix} 
                        0 & 1 \\
                        0 & 0
                    \end{matrix} \right)
                    \\[5pt]
                & = \hbar | \uparrow \ \rangle \langle \ \downarrow |
            \end{aligned}
            \hspace{18pt}
            \begin{aligned}
                S_- & = \hbar
                    \left( \begin{matrix} 
                        0 & 0 \\
                        1 & 0
                    \end{matrix} \right)
                    \\[5pt]
                & = \hbar | \downarrow \ \rangle \langle \ \uparrow |
            \end{aligned}
            \hspace{10pt} 
            \big(\hs \begin{gathered}
                \text{\scriptsize can't}\\[-10pt]
                \text{\scriptsize measure}
            \end{gathered} \hs\big)
            \hspace{10pt}
            \mss{ \begin{gathered}
                \text{Lad. Op. (see harm.)}\\[2pt]
                \begin{aligned}
                        [S_+, S_-] & = (2\hbar) S_z\\
                        [S_z, S_\pm] & = (\pm \hbar) S_+\\
                    \end{aligned} 
            \end{gathered} }
        \\[35pt]
    % S_z
    \left. \begin{aligned}
            S_z | \uparrow \ \rangle = \tfrac{\hbar}{2} | \uparrow \ \rangle \\[10pt]
            S_z | \downarrow \ \rangle = - \tfrac{\hbar}{2} | \downarrow \ \rangle \\
        \end{aligned} \hspace{18pt} \right\} 
        & \Rightarrow
        & \begin{aligned}
                S_z & = \dfrac{\hbar}{2}
                    \left( \begin{matrix} 
                        1 & 0 \\
                        0 & -1
                    \end{matrix} \right) 
                    = \dfrac{\hbar}{2} \sigma_z =
                    * \left( \begin{matrix} 
                        1 & 0 \\
                        0 & 1
                    \end{matrix} \right)
                    \left( \begin{matrix} 
                        \tfrac{\hbar}{2} & 0 \\
                        0 & -\tfrac{\hbar}{2}
                    \end{matrix} \right)
                    \left( \begin{matrix} 
                        1 & 0 \\
                        0 & 1
                    \end{matrix} \right)^{T*} 
                    \\[5pt]
                & = \tfrac{\hbar}{2} | \uparrow\ \rangle \langle \ \uparrow | 
                    - \tfrac{\hbar}{2} | \downarrow\ \rangle \langle \ \downarrow |
            \end{aligned}
        \\[35pt]
    % S_x, S_y
    \left. \begin{gathered}
            S_x = \tfrac{1}{2} (S_+ + S_-) \\[10pt]
            S_y = \tfrac{1}{2i} (S_+ - S_-)
        \end{gathered} \hspace{18pt} \right\} 
        & \Rightarrow
        & \begin{gathered}
            S_x = \frac{\hbar}{2}
                \left( \begin{matrix} 
                    0 & 1 \\
                    1 & 0
                \end{matrix} \right) = \dfrac{\hbar}{2} \sigma_x
                \hspace{18pt}
                S_y = \frac{\hbar}{2}
                \left( \begin{matrix} 
                    0 & -i \\
                    i & 0
                \end{matrix} \right) = \dfrac{\hbar}{2} \sigma_y 
                \\[5pt]
            % Anticommutator
            \mss{ \boxed{ \left\{ S_i, S_j \right\} = \tfrac{\hbar^2}{2} \delta_{ij} } }
                \hspace{20pt} (\text{\scriptsize only for \(s=1/2\) systems})
            \end{gathered}
\end{array}\)

% Pauli Matricies Properties
\vspace{25pt}
\noindent
\(
    \begin{aligned}[t]
        & \text{\underline{Properties of Pauli Matrices, \(\sigma_i\)}} \\[10pt]
        & \bullet\ \sigma_i = \sigma_i^{\dagger} = \sigma_i^{-1}\\
        & \ast\ \sigma_i^2 = {1}
            = (\hat{n} \cdot \sigma)^2 
            \leftrightarrow \mss{ \begin{aligned}
                & ( \hat{n} \cdot \sigma + \mathbbm{1} ) ( \hat{n} \cdot \sigma - \mathbbm{1} ) = 0 \\
                & ( \hat{n} \cdot S + \tfrac{\hbar}{2} ) ( \hat{n} \cdot S - \tfrac{\hbar}{2} ) 
                    = ( S_z + \tfrac{\hbar}{2} ) ( S_z - \tfrac{\hbar}{2} )
            \end{aligned} }
            \\[5pt]
        & \bullet\ \sigma_i \sigma_j = - \sigma_j \sigma_i = i \sigma_k = (\sigma_j \sigma_i)^\dagger
            \ \Rightarrow\ 
            \left[ \tfrac{\sigma_i}{2i}, \tfrac{\sigma_j}{2i} \right] = \tfrac{\sigma_k}{2i}
            \\
        & \ast\ \mss{ (A \cdot \sigma)(B \cdot \sigma) = A \cdot B + i (A \times B) \cdot \sigma }
            \hspace{20pt} ( \mss{ \text{\scriptsize if } \left[A_i, \sigma_i\right] = 0 = \left[B_i, \sigma_i\right] } )
            \\
        & \ast\ (\sigma_i \sigma_j)^2 = -1 \\
        & \ast\ (\sigma_i \sigma_j \sigma_k)^2 = -1 = \mathbbm{i}^2
            \\[5pt]
        & \bullet\ \text{Tr } \sigma_i = 0
            \ \Rightarrow\ 
            \text{Tr} (\sigma_\alpha \sigma_\beta) = 2 \delta_{\alpha\beta} 
            \hspace{15pt} \mss{\alpha \in (0, x, y, z)}
            \\
        & \ast\ \mss{ \sum } c_\alpha \sigma_\alpha = 0 
            \rightarrow
            c_\alpha = 0
            \ \Rightarrow\ 
            M_{2\times 2} = \mss{ \sum \tfrac{1}{2} \text{\scriptsize Tr}(M \sigma_\alpha) } \hs \sigma_\alpha
            \\[5pt]
        & \bullet\ \det(\sigma_i) = -1
    \end{aligned}
    \hfill
    \begin{aligned}[t]
        & \text{\underline{Gamma Matrices, \(\gamma_\alpha\)}}\\[10pt]
        & \bullet\ \gamma_i = \mss{\left[\arraycolsep=2pt\begin{matrix}
                0 & \sigma_i \\
                -\sigma_i & 0
            \end{matrix}\right]}
            , \ 
            \gamma_t = \mss{\left[\arraycolsep=2pt\begin{matrix}
                0 & \mathbbm{1} \\
                \mathbbm{1} & 0
            \end{matrix}\right]}
            \text{\scriptsize\ or }
            \mss{\left[\arraycolsep=2pt\begin{matrix}
                \mathbbm{1} & 0\\
                0 & - \mathbbm{1}
            \end{matrix}\right]}
            \\[5pt]
        & \ast\ \gamma_t^2 = {1} :\ e^{j\phi} = \cosh\phi + \gamma_t\sinh\phi\\[5pt]
        & \ast\ \gamma_x^2 = \gamma_y^2 = \gamma_z^2 = -1\\[5pt]
        & \bullet\ - \gamma_i = \gamma_i^\dagger = \gamma_i^{-1} \ , \ \gamma_t = \gamma_t^\dagger = \gamma_t^{-1}\\[5pt]
        & \bullet\ \gamma_\alpha \gamma_\beta = - \gamma_\beta \gamma_\alpha \\[5pt]
        & \ast\ (\gamma_i\gamma_j)^\dagger = \gamma_j \gamma_i\ , \ (\gamma_t\gamma_i)^\dagger = - \gamma_i \gamma_t \\[5pt]
        & \ast\ (\gamma_i\gamma_j)^2 = -1\ ,\ (\gamma_t\gamma_i)^2 = 1\\
        & \ast\ (\gamma_i\gamma_j\gamma_k)^2 = 1\ ,\ (\gamma_t\gamma_i\gamma_k)^2 = -1\\
        & \ast\ (\gamma_t \gamma_x \gamma_y \gamma_z)^2 = -1 = \mathbbm{i}^2
    \end{aligned}
\)

%--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
%
%
%
\newpage
% General Direction; Bloch Sphere
\noindent
\underline{General Direction, \(\hat{n}\), on Bloch Sphere (\(1, \theta, \phi\)) 
    \(\Leftrightarrow\) Pauli Vector, \(V\) (see Properties of \(\sigma_i\))}
    \\[10pt]
\(
    \begin{aligned}
        \hat{n} \cdot \vec{S} & = \cos\phi \sin\theta \hs S_x + \sin\phi \sin\theta \hs S_y + \cos\theta \hs S_z 
            = \boxed{ 
                \tfrac{\hbar}{2} \mss{ \left[\arraycolsep=2pt\begin{matrix}
                    n_z & n_x - i n_y \\
                    n_x + i n_y & - n_z
                \end{matrix}\right] } 
                = \tfrac{\hbar}{2} \mss{ \left[\arraycolsep=3pt\begin{matrix}
                        \cos\theta & \sin\theta e^{-i\phi} \\
                        \sin\theta e^{i\phi} & - \cos\theta
                    \end{matrix}\right] }
            }
            = V_{\hat{n}}
    \end{aligned}
\)

% Pauli Vector Properties
\vspace{10pt}\noindent
\(\begin{aligned}
    & \bullet\ V_{\vec{n}}^2 = \lVert \hsvec{n} \rVert^2 I
        \hspace{12pt} \bullet\ \det(V_{\vec{n}}) = - \lVert \hsvec{n}\hs \rVert^2
        \hspace{8pt} \bullet\ V = V^\dagger
        \hspace{8pt} \bullet\ \text{Tr} (V) = 0
        \hspace{8pt} \bullet\ \begin{gathered}
            \text{\scriptsize Reflect \(V\)}\\[-9pt]
            \text{\scriptsize over \(R_{\hat{n}} \perp\)}
        \end{gathered} : -RVR^{\bcancel{-1}}
        \\[2pt]
    & \bullet\ \begin{gathered}
            \text{\scriptsize Rotate \(V\) in}\\[-9pt]
            \text{\scriptsize \(xy\)-plane by \(\psi\)}
        \end{gathered} : 
        -[\mss{ \cos\tfrac{\psi}{2} \sigma_x + \sin\tfrac{\psi}{2} \sigma_y }][-\sigma_x V \sigma_x][..]
        = \underline{ [\mss{ \cos\tfrac{\psi}{2} \mathbbm{1} - \sin\tfrac{\psi}{2} \sigma_x \sigma_y }] V [..]^{\underline{-1}} }
        = \boxed{ \mss{(\pm)} U V \mss{(\pm)} U^\dagger}
        \hspace{15pt}
        ( \mss{ U \in SU(2) } )
        \\[8pt]
    & \bullet\ i \hsvec{n} \cdot \sigma \ =\ i n_x \sigma_x + i n_y \sigma_y + i n_z \sigma_z 
        \ =\ n_x \sigma_y \sigma_z + n_y \sigma_z \sigma_x + n_z \sigma_x \sigma_y 
\end{aligned}\)

% Eigenvector of Pauli Matrix/Vector
\vspace{10pt}\noindent
\(
    \ast\ \
    \hat{n} \cdot \vec{S} \hs\hs | \chi_\pm \rangle = \mss{\pm} \tfrac{\hbar}{2} \hs | \chi_\pm \rangle
    \ \Rightarrow\ 
    \boxed{
        | \chi_+ \rangle = \mss{
            e^{i\gamma}
            \left[\begin{matrix}
                \cos\tfrac{\theta}{2} \hs e^{- i \phi/2}\\[5pt]
                \sin\tfrac{\theta}{2} \hs e^{i \phi/2}
            \end{matrix}\right]
        }
        = \mss{
            \left[\begin{matrix}
                1\\[5pt]
                \tan\tfrac{\theta}{2} \hs e^{i \phi}
            \end{matrix}\right]
        }
        \ , \
        | \chi_- \rangle = \mss{
            e^{i\gamma}
            \left[\begin{matrix}
                - \sin\tfrac{\theta}{2} \hs e^{- i \phi/2}\\[5pt]
                \cos\tfrac{\theta}{2} \hs e^{i \phi/2}
            \end{matrix}\right]
        }
        = \mss{
            \left[\begin{matrix}
                1\\[5pt]
                -\cot\tfrac{\theta}{2} \hs e^{i \phi}
            \end{matrix}\right]
        }
    }
\)

% Riemann Sphere to Complex Projected Line
\vspace{10pt}\noindent
\(\ast\ \ \)\underline{Riemann Sphere \(\rightarrow \mathbb{C}P^1\)}: \ \(
    |\chi\rangle 
    = \mss{ \left[ \begin{matrix}
        1\\ 
        f (\theta,\phi)
    \end{matrix} \right] } 
    \rightarrow 
    \left. \begin{aligned}
        f \mss{(\theta,\phi)} \in \mss{(-\infty, \infty)}:
            && 0 & \leq \theta < \pi
            \\
        f \mss{(\theta,\phi)} \in \mss{(-\infty, \infty)}:
            && \pi & \leq \theta < 2\pi
    \end{aligned} \right\}
    \ \ (\text{\scriptsize double cover})
\)

% Projectors and Nilpotents
\vspace{15pt}\noindent
\underline{Projectors and Nilpotents}:\\[10pt]
% Projectors
\(
    \begin{aligned}
        P^\pm_U & = \tfrac{1}{2}(1 \pm U)\\
        & \mss{(U^2 = 1)} 
            \\[5pt]
        P_z^\pm & = \tfrac{\bcancel{\sigma_z}}{2}(1 \pm \sigma_z)^{\bcancel{\dagger}} \bcancel{\sigma_z}\\
        & = | \pm \rangle = | z^\pm \rangle 
            \\[5pt]
        P_{tz}^\pm & = \tfrac{\bcancel{\gamma_t\gamma_z}}{2}(1 \pm \gamma_t\gamma_z) \bcancel{\gamma_t\gamma_z}
    \end{aligned}
    \hfill\vline\hfill
    \begin{aligned}
        | \xi \rangle & =
            \left[ \begin{matrix}
                a + bi & 0 \\
                c + di & 0
            \end{matrix} \right] 
            = \boxed{ (a P_z^+ + b \sigma_x \sigma_y P_z^+) + (c \sigma_x P_z^+ + d \sigma_y P_z^+ ) }
            \\[5pt]
        | \xi \rangle \langle \chi | & =
            \mss{ \arraycolsep=2pt \left[ \begin{matrix}
                z & x - iy\\
                x + iy & -z
            \end{matrix} \right] }
            = \xi \xi^T \epsilon
            = \mss{
            \left[ \begin{matrix}
                \xi^1 & 0 \\
                \xi^2 & 0
            \end{matrix} \right] 
            \left[ \begin{matrix}
                - \xi^2 & \xi^1 \\
                0 & 0
            \end{matrix} \right] 
            }
            \hspace{20pt}
            \mss{ %\begin{gathered}
                \det \left( | \xi \rangle \langle \chi | \right) = 0 
                \ , \ 
                \epsilon = \left[ \arraycolsep=2pt \begin{matrix}
                        0 & 1 \\
                        -1 & 0
                    \end{matrix}\right]
            %\end{gathered} 
            }
            \\[5pt]
        & = x \sigma_x + y \sigma_y + z \sigma_z 
            = \Big( \xi^1 | z^+ \rangle + \xi^2 \sigma_x| z^+ \rangle \Big)
            \Big( \nhs\nhs -\xi^2 \langle z^+ |^* + \xi^1 \sigma_x \langle z^+ |^* \Big)
    \end{aligned}
\)

\vspace{15pt}\noindent
% Nilpotents
\(
    \begin{aligned}
        \{ \alpha_\pm, \alpha_\pm \} & = 0
            \\[8pt]
        \{ \alpha_{-}, \alpha_{+} \} & = 1 \\
        \alpha_{-} \alpha_+ + \alpha_+ \alpha_{-} & = P_+ + P_{-}
            \\[8pt]
        P_\pm P_\mp = 0 & = P_\mp P_\pm
    \end{aligned}\
    \hspace{10pt}\vline\hspace{10pt}
    \begin{gathered}
        \alpha_{UV}^\pm = \tfrac{1}{2}( U + V ) \hspace{20pt} \mss{(U^2 = 1 \ ,\ V^2 = -1)}\\[10pt]
        Cl(1,3,\mathbb{C}) :\
            \begin{aligned}
                a_{tz}^\pm & = \tfrac{1}{2}( \gamma_t + \gamma_z ) \hspace{-5pt}
                    && \Rightarrow\ P_{tz}^\pm = a_{tz}^\mp a_{tz}^\pm = \tfrac{1}{2}(1 \pm \gamma_t \gamma_z)
                    \\[5pt]
                b_{ixy}^\pm & = \tfrac{1}{2}( i\gamma_x + \gamma_y ) \hspace{-5pt}
                    && \Rightarrow\ P_{ixy}^\pm = b_{ixy}^\mp b_{ixy}^\pm = \tfrac{1}{2}(1 \pm i\gamma_x \gamma_y)
            \end{aligned}
            \\[10pt]
        \begin{aligned}
            \{ a_\pm, b_\pm \} & = 0 = \{ a_\pm, b_\mp \} \\
            \left[ P_{tz}^\pm , P_{ixy}^\pm \right] & = 0 = \left[ P_{tz}^\pm , P_{ixy}^\mp \right]
            \end{aligned}
            \ \rightarrow \ \boxed{ 
                | \epsilon \rangle = \epsilon^1 P_{tz}^+ P_{ixy}^+ + \epsilon^2 \alpha_{tzixy}^+ P_{tz}^+ P_{ixy}^+
            }
    \end{gathered}
\)

% Lie Groups and Algebras
\vspace{20pt}\noindent
% Line
\hrulefill

\vspace{20pt}\noindent
% SO(3)
\(
    \begin{aligned}
        & \underline{R \in SO(3) \sim \mathbb{R}P^3} :\ \begin{aligned}
                & R\mss{(\theta)} = e^{\theta g} \\[-2pt]
                & R\mss{(0)} = \mathbbm{1}
            \end{aligned}
            % Algebra g
            \ \Rightarrow\ \left. \tfrac{dR}{d\theta} \right|_{\theta = 0} 
            = \boxed{ 
                g[R] \in 
                \begin{aligned}
                    & \mathfrak{so}\mss{(3)} \\[-2pt]
                    & \mathfrak{su}\mss{(2)} 
                \end{aligned}
            }
            \\[5pt]
        % Properties
        & \bullet\ \det{( R=e^{\theta g} )} = 1 = e^{\theta\hs \text{Tr}(g)}\ \Rightarrow\ \boxed{ \text{Tr}(g) = 0 }\\
        & \bullet\ \boxed{ \mss{ \begin{gathered}
                v^T [R^T R] v = v^T \mathbbm{1} v \\
                R^T = R^{-1}
            \end{gathered} } } \ \Rightarrow\ g^T + g = 0 \ \leftrightarrow\ \boxed{ g^T = - g}
            \\
    \end{aligned}
    \hspace{15pt}\vline\hspace{15pt}
    % Commutation
    \begin{aligned}
        [g_{yz}, g_{zx}] & = g_{xy} \equiv g_z = [g_{x}, g_{y}] \\
        [g_{zx}, g_{xy}] & = g_{yz} \equiv g_x = [g_{y}, g_{z}] \\
        [g_{xy}, g_{yz}] & = g_{zx} \equiv g_y = [g_{z}, g_{x}] 
    \end{aligned}
\)

%-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
%
%
%
\newpage
\noindent
% SU(2) matrices
\(\begin{aligned}
    & \underline{ 
        \begin{aligned}
            & U \in SU(2) = 2 \times SO(3) = Spin(3)\\
            & = \mss{ \begin{gathered}
                    2n \text{ grade},\\[-2pt]
                    \lVert \pm U_i \rVert^2 = \mathbbm{1}
                \end{gathered} 
                }
                \in Cl(3,0)
                \sim S^3_{phere}
        \end{aligned} 
        } :\ 
        \boxed{ 
            \mss{ 
            \left[ \arraycolsep=2pt \begin{matrix}
                \alpha & - \beta^*\\
                \beta & \alpha^*
            \end{matrix} \right] 
            }
            % Exponential Map
            \mss{ \begin{aligned}
                & = e^{ - i \tfrac{\psi}{2} \hat{n} \cdot \sigma } 
                    = \cos\tfrac{\psi}{2} \mathbbm{1} - \sin\tfrac{\psi}{2} \hs \mathbbm{i}\hs \hsvec{n} \cdot \sigma
                    \\
                & \sim\ e^{ - \tfrac{\psi}{2} \sigma_i \sigma_j } 
                    = \cos\tfrac{\psi}{2} \mathbbm{1} - \sin\tfrac{\psi}{2} \hs \sigma_i \sigma_j
            \end{aligned} }
        }
        % Algebra g
        \ \Rightarrow\ \boxed{ 
            g[U] \in 
            \begin{aligned}
                & \mathfrak{su}\mss{(2)} \\[-2pt]
                & \mathfrak{so}\mss{(3)}
            \end{aligned}
        }
        \\[5pt]
    % Examples of U
    & \begin{aligned}
            & \bullet\ \mss{ \begin{gathered}
                    \text{Rotate \(\hat{k}\) to \(\hat{k}'\) by angle \(\theta\)}\\[-3pt]
                    \hat{\theta} = (-\sin\phi, \cos\phi, 0) = \hat{k} \times \hat{k}' 
                \end{gathered} }
                && \hspace{10pt}
                \underline{ 
                    U[R(\theta)] = \cos \tfrac{\theta}{2} \mathbbm{1} - \sin \tfrac{\theta}{2} i \big( \hat{\theta} \cdot \sigma \big) 
                }
                = \mss{ \left[\begin{matrix}
                    \cos \tfrac{\theta}{2} & - \sin \tfrac{\theta}{2} \hs e^{- i \phi}\\[3pt]
                    \sin \tfrac{\theta}{2} \hs e^{i \phi} & \cos \tfrac{\theta}{2}
                \end{matrix}\right] }
                \\[5pt]
            & \bullet\ \mss{ \begin{gathered}
                    \text{Rotate about \(\hat{\psi}\) by angle \(\psi\)}\\[-3pt]
                    \hat{\psi} = \hat{n} = (n^x, n^y, n^z) 
                \end{gathered} }
                && \hspace{10pt}
                \underline{ U[R(\psi)] = \cos \tfrac{\psi}{2} \mathbbm{1} - \sin \tfrac{\psi}{2} i \big( \hat{\psi} \cdot \sigma \big) }
                = \mss{ \left[\begin{matrix}
                    \cos \tfrac{\psi}{2} - i n^z \sin \tfrac{\psi}{2}  & (- i n^x - n^y) \sin \tfrac{\psi}{2} \\[3pt]
                    (- i n^x + n^y) \sin \tfrac{\psi}{2} & \cos \tfrac{\psi}{2} + i n^z \sin \tfrac{\psi}{2}
                \end{matrix}\right] }
        \end{aligned}
        \\[5pt]
    % Properties
    & \begin{aligned}
            & \bullet\ \det(U) = \alpha^*\alpha + \beta^*\beta = 1 \ \Rightarrow\ \boxed{ \text{Tr}(g) = 0 }\\
            & \bullet\ 
                \boxed{ \mss{ \begin{gathered}
                    \xi^\dagger [U^\dagger U] \chi = \xi^\dagger \mathbbm{1} \chi \\
                    U^\dagger = U^{-1} 
                \end{gathered} } }
                \ \Rightarrow\ g^\dagger  + g = 0 \ \leftrightarrow\ \boxed{ g^\dagger = -g }
                \\
            & \bullet\ \boxed{ V' = \mss{(\pm)} U V \mss{(\pm)} U^\dagger = U [ v v^T \epsilon ] U^{-1}}
                \ , \ \begin{gathered}
                    \epsilon = \mss{ \arraycolsep=2pt \left[ \begin{matrix}
                            0 & 1\\
                            -1 & 0
                        \end{matrix} \right] }\\
                    \mss{(\det vv^T = 0)}
                \end{gathered}
        \end{aligned}
        \hspace{15pt}\vline\hspace{15pt}
        % Commutation
        \begin{aligned}
            - \tfrac{1}{2} \sigma_x \sigma_y & = g_{xy} = [g_{yz}, g_{zx}] 
                = - \tfrac{\mathbbm{i}}{2} \sigma_z = \tfrac{1}{2}\hs \hs \hat{\nhs i}
                \\
            - \tfrac{1}{2} \sigma_y \sigma_z & = g_{yz} = [g_{zx}, g_{xy}] 
                = - \tfrac{\mathbbm{i}}{2} \sigma_x = \tfrac{1}{2}\hs \hs \hs \hat{\nhs \nhs j}
                \\
            - \tfrac{1}{2} \sigma_z \sigma_x & = g_{zx} = [g_{xy}, g_{yz}] 
                = - \tfrac{\mathbbm{i}}{2} \sigma_y = \tfrac{1}{2}\hs \hat{k}
        \end{aligned}
\end{aligned}\)

\vspace{15pt}\noindent
% SO+(3)
\(
    \begin{aligned}
        & \underline{\Lambda \in SO^+(1,3)} :\ \begin{aligned}
                & \Lambda\mss{(\theta)} = e^{\theta g} \\[-2pt]
                & \Lambda\mss{(0)} = \mathbbm{1}
            \end{aligned}
            % Algebra g
            \ \Rightarrow\ \left. \tfrac{d\Lambda}{d\theta} \right|_{\theta = 0} 
            = \boxed{ 
                g[\Lambda] \in 
                \begin{aligned}
                    & \mathfrak{so^+}\mss{(1,3)}\\[-2pt]
                    & \mathfrak{sl}\mss{(2,\mathbb{C})}
                \end{aligned}
            }
            \\[5pt]
        % Properties
        & \begin{aligned}
                & \bullet\ \boxed{ \mss{ 
                        v^T [\eta] v = v^T [\Lambda^T \eta \Lambda] v = v^T \eta \Lambda^{-1} \nhs\cdot\nhs \Lambda v
                    } }
                    \ \Rightarrow\ \boxed{ g^T = -\eta g \eta }
                    \ , \ \mss{\eta = (+,-,-,-)}
                    \\[5pt]
                & \hs\hs\hs \begin{aligned}
                        & \bullet &\text{\scriptsize Rotation},\ J_{ij} & :\ \boxed{ \Lambda_{ij}^T = \Lambda_{ij}^{-1} }
                            \ \Rightarrow\ \boxed{ \text{Tr}(J) = 0 ,\ J^T = -J}
                            \\
                        & \bullet &\text{\scriptsize Boost},\ K_{ti} & :\ \boxed{ \Lambda_{ti}^T = \Lambda_{ti} }
                            \ \Rightarrow\ \boxed{ \text{Tr}(K) = 0 ,\ K^T = K}
                    \end{aligned}
            \end{aligned}
            \\
    \end{aligned}
    \hspace{15pt}\vline\hspace{15pt}
    % Commutation
    \left.
    \begin{aligned}
        [J_{yz}, J_{zx}] & = J_{xy}\\
        [K_{tx}, K_{ty}] & = -J_{xy}
            \\[5pt]
        [J_{yz}, K_{ty}] & = K_{tz}\\
        [J_{yz}, K_{tz}] & = -K_{ty}
    \end{aligned}
    \hspace{5pt}\right\}
    \times 3
\)

% SL(2,C) matrices
\vspace{15pt}\noindent
\(\begin{aligned}
    & \underline{ 
        \begin{aligned}
            & L \in SL(2, \mathbb{C}) = 2 \times SO^+(1,3) = \\
            & Spin \mss{(1,3)} = \ \subset Cl \mss{(3,0)} = \ \subset Cl \mss{(1,3)}
        \end{aligned} 
        } :\ 
        \boxed{ 
            \mss{ 
            \left[ \arraycolsep=2pt \begin{matrix}
                \alpha & \beta\\
                \gamma & \alpha^*
            \end{matrix} \right] 
            }
            \sim
            % Exponential Map
            \begin{aligned}
                e^{ \theta J_{ij} } & = 
                    \mss{ \begin{aligned}
                        & \cos\tfrac{\psi}{2} \mathbbm{1} - \sin\tfrac{\psi}{2} \hs \sigma_i \sigma_j\\
                        & \cos\tfrac{\psi}{2} \mathbbm{1} + \sin\tfrac{\psi}{2} \hs \gamma_i \gamma_j
                    \end{aligned} }
                    \\
                e^{ \theta K_{ti} } & = 
                    \mss{ \begin{aligned}
                        & \cosh \tfrac{\psi}{2} \mathbbm{1} - \sinh\tfrac{\psi}{2} \hs \sigma_i\\
                        & \cosh \tfrac{\psi}{2} \mathbbm{1} + \sinh\tfrac{\psi}{2} \hs \gamma_i
                    \end{aligned} }
            \end{aligned}
        }
        % Algebra g
        \ \Rightarrow\ \boxed{ 
            g[L] \in 
            \begin{aligned}
                & \mathfrak{sl}\mss{(2,\mathbb{C})} = \mathfrak{so^+}\mss{(1,3)} \\[-2pt]
                & \mathfrak{su}\mss{(2)} \oplus \mss{(\mp^l_r i)} \hs \mathfrak{su}\mss{(2)} \\[-2pt]
                & \mathfrak{su}\mss{(2)}_\mathbb{C}
            \end{aligned} 
        }
        \\[5pt]
    % Properties
    & \begin{aligned}
            & \begin{aligned}
                    & \bullet\ \boxed{ \mss{
                        \begin{gathered}
                            \psi^T [\epsilon] \phi = \psi^T [L^T \epsilon L] \phi = \psi^T \epsilon L^{-1} \nhs \cdot \nhs L \phi\\
                            = - \phi^T \epsilon \psi = 0 \ \ \text{\scriptsize if \ \(\psi = \phi\)} 
                        \end{gathered}
                        } }
                        \ \Rightarrow\ \boxed{ g^T \epsilon = - \epsilon g }
                        \ , \ \mss{ \arraycolsep=2pt \epsilon = \left[ \begin{matrix}
                            0 & 1\\
                            -1 & 0
                        \end{matrix} \right] }
                        \\[5pt]
                    & \hs\hs\hs \begin{aligned}
                            &\bullet &\text{\scriptsize Rotation},\ J_{ij} & :\ \boxed{ L_{ij}^\dagger = L_{ij}^{-1} }
                                \ \Rightarrow\ \boxed{ \text{Tr}(J) = 0 ,\ J^T = -J}
                                \\
                            &\bullet &\text{\scriptsize Boost},\ K_{ti} & :\ \boxed{ L_{ti}^\dagger = L_{ti} }
                                \ \Rightarrow\ \boxed{ \text{Tr}(K) = 0 ,\ K^T = K}
                        \end{aligned}
                        \\[5pt]
                \end{aligned}
                \hspace{5pt}\vline\hspace{5pt}
                % Commutation
                \begin{aligned}
                    [J_{yz}, J_{zx}] & = J_{xy} 
                        = - \tfrac{1}{2} \sigma_x \sigma_y \rightarrow \tfrac{1}{2} \gamma_x \gamma_y
                        \\
                    [K_{tx}, K_{ty}] & = -J_{xy}
                        \\[5pt]
                    [J_{yz}, K_{ty}] & = K_{tz} 
                        = \mp^l_r \tfrac{1}{2} \sigma_z \rightarrow \pm^l_r \tfrac{1}{2} \gamma_t \gamma_z
                        \\
                    [J_{yz}, K_{tz}] & = -K_{ty}
                \end{aligned}
                \\[5pt]
            % Left and Right Chiral
            & \bullet\ \text{\scriptsize Left/Left Dual}:\
                \mss{ \arraycolsep=1pt \begin{array}{r c c c}
                    w_{ld} \cdot w_l: & \psi^T \epsilon \cdot \phi & = & \psi^T \epsilon L^{-1} \nhs \cdot \nhs L \phi \\[3pt]
                    w_{ld}^T: & - \epsilon \psi & \rightarrow & [L^T]^{-1} [- \epsilon \psi] \\
                \end{array} }
                \hspace{15pt}
                \bullet\ \text{\scriptsize Right Dual/Right}:\
                \mss{ \arraycolsep=1pt \begin{array}{r c c c}
                    w_r \cdot w_{rd}:& \psi^\dagger \epsilon \cdot \phi^* & =
                        & \psi^\dagger \epsilon [L^*]^{-1} \nhs\cdot\nhs L^* \phi^*\\[3pt] 
                    w_r^T: & - \epsilon \psi^* & \rightarrow & [L^\dagger]^{-1} [- \epsilon \psi^*] \\
                \end{array} }
                \\[5pt]
            % Weyl Vector Rotation
            & \bullet\ \boxed{ \mss{
                    W' = \mss{(\pm)} L W \mss{(\pm)} L^\dagger = L [ w_l w_l^\dagger ] [(L^\dagger)^{-1}]^{-1} 
                    \ =\ L_{ij} [ w_l w_{rd} ] L_{ij}^{-1} \ \ \text{\scriptsize or}\ \ L_{ti} [ w_l w_{rd} ] [L_{ti}^{-1}]^{-1}
                } }
                \hspace{20pt} \mss{(\det w_l w_l^\dagger = 0)}
                \\[5pt]
            & \begin{aligned}[t]
                    % Direct Sum
                    & \bullet\ \underline{ (\tfrac{1}{2},0) \oplus (0,\tfrac{1}{2}) }:\ 
                        \mss{ \arraycolsep=2pt \left[ \begin{matrix}
                            L & 0\\
                            0 & [L^\dagger]^{-1}
                        \end{matrix} \right] 
                        \left[ \begin{matrix}
                            w_l\\
                            w_r^T
                        \end{matrix} \right]} 
                        \\[10pt]
                    % Direct Product
                    & \bullet\ \underline{ \mss{ (\tfrac{1}{2},0) \otimes (0,\tfrac{1}{2}) = (\tfrac{1}{2},\tfrac{1}{2}) } } :\ 
                        \mss{ \arraycolsep=2pt 
                        \left[ \begin{matrix}
                            c \hs\tilde{\nhs t}\\
                            \tilde{r}
                        \end{matrix} \hs\hs \right] 
                        }
                        =
                        \mss{ \arraycolsep=2pt 
                            [ A^{-1} L \otimes [L^\dagger]^{-1} A ]
                            \left[ \begin{matrix}
                                ct\\
                                \hsvec{r}
                            \end{matrix} \right]
                            = [SO(3)]
                            \left[ \begin{matrix}
                                ct\\
                                \hsvec{r}
                            \end{matrix} \right]
                            } 
                \end{aligned}
                \hspace{20pt}
                % Complexified
                \bullet\ \begin{gathered}[t]
                    \mathfrak{sl}(2,\mathbb{C})_\mathbb{C} = \mathfrak{su}(2)_\mathbb{C} \oplus \mathfrak{su}(2)_\mathbb{C}:\\[5pt]
                    A_i^\pm = \tfrac{1}{2} (J_{jk} \pm K_{ti})\\
                    [A_i^\pm, A_j^\pm] = A_k^\pm \ \ , \ \ [A^+, A^-] = 0
                \end{gathered}
        \end{aligned}
\end{aligned}\)

%-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

\newpage
% su(2) Rep for Raising/Lowering Operators
\noindent
\underline{\(\mathfrak{su}(2)\) Representations for Generators (Raising/Lowering)}\\[10pt]
\(
    % g_+ and g_-
    \begin{aligned}
        g_+ & = i g_{yz} - g_{zx} \\
        & = \mss{ \left[ \begin{matrix}
                0 & 1\\
                0 & 0        
            \end{matrix} \right] }
            = \tfrac{1}{2} \sigma_x + \tfrac{i}{2} \sigma_y 
            \\[5pt]
        g_- & = i g_{yz} + g_{zx} \\
        & = \mss{ \left[ \begin{matrix}
                0 & 0\\
                1 & 0        
            \end{matrix} \right] }
            = \tfrac{1}{2} \sigma_x - \tfrac{i}{2} \sigma_y 
    \end{aligned}
    \hspace{25pt}
    % g_z and g^2
    \begin{aligned}
        g_z & = i g_{xy} 
            = ``\tfrac{1}{2}" \mss{ \arraycolsep=3pt \left[ \begin{matrix}
                1 & 0\\
                0 & -1
            \end{matrix} \right] }
            = \tfrac{1}{2} \sigma_z
            \\[10pt]
        g^2 & = - \left( g_{yz}^2 + g_{zx}^2 + g_{xy}^2 \right)\\[2pt]
        & \mss{ \left( \begin{gathered}
                \text{Casimir Op. in }\\[-4pt]
                % \text{\scriptsize not in \( \mathfrak{su}(2) \)}\\[-6pt]
                \text{Universal Env. Alg.}
            \end{gathered} \right) }
    \end{aligned}
    \ \Rightarrow \
    % Commutation relations
    \begin{gathered}
        \begin{aligned}
                \left[ g_+, g_- \right] & = 2g_z\\
                \left[ g_z, g_\pm \right] & = \pm g_\pm\\
                \left[ g_{ij}, g^2 \right] & = 0
            \end{aligned}
            \\[7pt]
        g_\pm^\dagger g_\pm = g^2 - g_z^2 \mp g_z
    \end{gathered}
\)

\vspace{15pt}\noindent
% Eigenvalues
\(
    \Rightarrow\
    \begin{aligned}
        g_z | m \rangle & = m | m \rangle \\
        g_z \cdot g_\pm | m \rangle & = (m \pm 1) g_\pm | m \rangle \\[2pt]
        g^2 | j,m \rangle & = j(j+1) | j,m \rangle\\
    \end{aligned}
    \ \Rightarrow\ 
    \begin{aligned}
        g_\pm^\dagger g_\pm | j,m \rangle & = \Big[ j(j+1) - m (m\pm 1) \Big] | j,m \rangle\\
        g_\pm | j,m \rangle & = \boxed{ \sqrt{ j(j+1) - m (m\pm 1) } | j,m \rangle }\\
    \end{aligned}
\)

\vspace{10pt}\noindent
% Matrix Representations
\(
    \begin{aligned}
        \mathbbm{1}_3 = 
            \mss{ \arraycolsep=2pt \left[ \begin{matrix}
                | & | & |\\[2pt]
                | 1 \rangle & | 0 \rangle & | -1 \rangle \\[2pt]
                | & | & |
            \end{matrix} \right] }
    \end{aligned}
    \ , \ 
    \begin{aligned}
        \mathbbm{1}_4 = 
            \mss{ \arraycolsep=2pt \left[ \begin{matrix}
                | & | & | & |\\[2pt]
                | \tfrac{3}{2} \rangle & | \tfrac{1}{2} \rangle & | \tfrac{-1}{2} \rangle & | \tfrac{-3}{2} \rangle\\[2pt]
                | & | & | & |
            \end{matrix} \right] }
    \end{aligned}
    \ ,\ \dots \hspace{15pt}
    \begin{aligned}
        (\overline{g_{\pm}})_{ij} & = \langle i | g_{\pm} | j \rangle \\
        (\overline{g_{z}})_{ij} & = \langle i | g_{z} | j \rangle 
    \end{aligned}
    \ \Rightarrow\ 
    \boxed{ \begin{aligned}
        \overline{ g_{yz} } & = \tfrac{1}{2i}( \overline{g_-} + \overline{g_+})\\
        \overline{ g_{zx} } & = \tfrac{1}{2i}( \overline{g_-} - \overline{g_+})\\
        \overline{ g_{yz} } & = -i \hs \overline{g_z}
    \end{aligned} }
\)

\vspace{15pt}
%------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
%------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
% 2 Particles w/ Spin 1/2
\subsection{2 Objects w/ Spin \ \ {\scriptsize Objects could be orbital momentum, another particle spin, etc.}}

\subsubsection{2 Objects w/ Spin \(\frac{1}{2}\):\ \ \
    \(
        \mss{\arraycolsep=1pt \begin{array}{r r c l c l}
            \text{Dim}:\ & 2 &\otimes& 2 &=& 3 \oplus 1\\
            \text{Spin}:\ & \tfrac{1}{2} &\otimes& \tfrac{1}{2} &=& 1 \oplus 0 
        \end{array} }
        \ \Rightarrow\ \mss{ \displaystyle (2s_1+1)(2s_2+1) = \sum_{s=|s_1-s_2|}^{s_1+s_2} 2s+1 } 
    \) 
}

\vspace{5pt}
*Find Eigenvectors, \(e_i\) , of \( ( S^{ (1,2) } )_z \) and 
    \( ( S^{ (1,2) } )^2 \) in the form of \( | \chi_i \chi_j \rangle \) ( using \( ( S^{ (1,2) } )_\pm \) )

\vspace{10pt}\noindent
% Tensor Product for 2 particles
\[ \boxed{  \chi_i \chi_j \rightarrow | \chi_i \chi_j \rangle \equiv | \chi_i \rangle | \chi_j \rangle 
    \equiv | \chi_i \rangle \otimes | \chi_j \rangle } \]

% Chi for 1 particle
\vspace{10pt} \noindent
Choose \( | \chi_i \rangle \equiv S_z\)-Eigenvector w/ 
    Spin \(\frac{1}{2}\) (e.g, \( | \frac{1}{2} \frac{-1}{2} \rangle 
        = \left( \begin{smallmatrix} 0 \\ 1 \end{smallmatrix} \right) \), 
        as opposed to \( \left( \begin{smallmatrix} .6 \\ .8 \end{smallmatrix} \right) \))

\vspace{10pt} \noindent
\begin{minipage}[t]{.5\textwidth}
    % "Vector" of Matrices
    \begin{center} \( 
        S^{(i)} \equiv 
        \left( \begin{matrix} 
            S^{(i)}_x\\[5pt] 
            S^{(i)}_y\\[5pt] 
            S^{(i)}_z 
        \end{matrix}\right) 
    \) \end{center}
        
    % Matrices only work on respective particles
    \( 
        \bullet \ S^{(2)}_z S^{(1)}_x \Big( | \chi_1 \rangle \otimes | \chi_2 \rangle \Big)
        = \left( S^{(1)}_x | \chi_1 \rangle \right) \otimes \left( S^{(2)}_z | \chi_2 \rangle \right) 
    \)\\[10pt]
    % Dot product for "vector" of matrices
    \( \begin{aligned}
        \bullet \ S^{(i)} \dotP S^{(j)} & \equiv \underline{ S^{(i)}_x S^{(j)}_x + S^{(i)}_y S^{(j)}_y } + S^{(i)}_z S^{(j)}_z \\[5pt]
        & = S^{(i)}_z S^{(j)}_z + \underline{ \tfrac{1}{2} S^{(i)}_+ S^{(j)}_- + \tfrac{1}{2} S^{(i)}_- S^{(j)}_+ }
            \\[5pt]
        ( S^{(i)} )^2 & \equiv S^{(i)} \dotP S^{(i)} 
    \end{aligned}\)
\end{minipage}
\hfill\vline\hfill
\begin{minipage}[t]{.45\textwidth}
    % Sum of "Vector" of Matrices
    \begin{center} \( 
        S^{(1,2)} \equiv \left( S^{(1)} + S^{(2)} \right) \equiv 
        \left( \begin{matrix} S^{(1)}_x + S^{(2)}_x \\[5pt]
            S^{(1)}_y + S^{(2)}_y \\[5pt]
            S^{(1)}_z + S^{(2)}_z 
        \end{matrix} \right) 
    \) \end{center}

    % \vspace{5pt}
    \( \bullet \ \left( S^{(1,2)} \right)^2 =
        \left( S^{(1)} + S^{(2)} \right) \dotP \left( S^{(1)} + S^{(2)} \right) \)
\end{minipage}

% 1.) Find Eigenvalues for S^(1,2)_z
\noindent
\textbf{1.} \(\left( S^{(1,2)} \right)_z\) \\[10pt]
\begin{minipage}[t]{.55\textwidth}
    \( \begin{aligned}[t] 
        \left( S^{(1,2)} \right)_z \chi_1 \chi_2 
            &= \Big( S^{(1)}_z + S^{(2)}_z \Big) 
                | \chi_1 \rangle | \chi_2 \rangle\\[10pt]
        &= S^{(1)}_z | \chi_1 \rangle \otimes | \chi_2 \rangle 
            + | \chi_1 \rangle \otimes S^{(2)}_z | \chi_2 \rangle \\[10pt]
        \left( S^{(1,2)} \right)_z  | \chi_1 \chi_2 \rangle 
            &= \hbar (m_1 + m_2) \ | \chi_1 \chi_2 \rangle
    \end{aligned} \)
    
    \vspace{10pt}
    \( \Rightarrow \ \underline{ e_i = a_i| \uparrow \uparrow \ \rangle + b_i| \uparrow \downarrow \ \rangle +
    c_i| \downarrow \uparrow \ \rangle + d_i| \downarrow \downarrow \ \rangle } \)    
\end{minipage}
\hfill\vline\hfill
\begin{minipage}[t]{.3\textwidth}
    \( \begin{aligned}[t]
        | \uparrow \uparrow \ \rangle \quad & =
            & | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{1}{2} \rangle 
            & \otimes | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{1}{2} \rangle 
            \\[10pt]
        | \uparrow \downarrow \ \rangle \quad & =
            & | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{1}{2} \rangle 
            & \otimes | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{-1}{2} \rangle 
            \\[10pt]
        | \downarrow \uparrow \ \rangle \quad & =
            & | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{-1}{2} \rangle 
            & \otimes | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{1}{2} \rangle 
            \\[10pt]
        | \downarrow \downarrow \ \rangle \quad & =
            & | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{-1}{2} \rangle 
            & \otimes | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{-1}{2} \rangle
    \end{aligned}  \)
\end{minipage}

    \\[10pt]

    & \hspace{18pt}\hspace{18pt}

e_i \in \left\{ \begin{gathered}

        { \setlength{\arraycolsep}{3pt} \begin{array}{c c c c c}
            | 1 \ 1 \rangle & =
                & \mss{1 \leftarrow\ } \bcancel{e^{i\phi}} \ | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{1}{2} \rangle | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{1}{2} \rangle 
                & =
                & | \uparrow \uparrow \ \rangle 
                \\[10pt]
            | 1 \ 0 \rangle & =
                & \tfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \Big(
                    | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{1}{2} \rangle | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{-1}{2} \rangle +
                    | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{-1}{2} \rangle | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{1}{2} \rangle \Big)
                & =
                & \tfrac{\sqrt{2}}{2} \big( | {\scriptstyle \uparrow \downarrow} \rangle +
                    | {\scriptstyle \downarrow \uparrow} \rangle \big)
                \\[10pt]
            | 1 \ \text{-}1 \rangle & =
                & | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{-1}{2} \rangle | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{-1}{2} \rangle
                & =
                & | \downarrow \downarrow \ \rangle
        \end{array} } 
        \right\} 
        \hspace{18pt} \text{Triplet}: \ s=1 
        \\[15pt]
    \left.
            { \setlength{\arraycolsep}{3pt}
            \begin{array}{c c c c c}
                | 0 \ 0 \rangle & =
                    & \tfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \Big( 
                        | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{1}{2} \rangle | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{-1}{2} \rangle -
                        | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{-1}{2} \rangle | \tfrac{1}{2} \tfrac{1}{2} \rangle \Big)
                    & =
                    & \tfrac{\sqrt{2}}{2} \big( | {\scriptstyle \uparrow \downarrow} \rangle - 
                        | {\scriptstyle \downarrow \uparrow} \rangle \big)
            \end{array} }
        \right\} 
        \hspace{18pt} \text{Singlet}: \ s=0 
\end{gathered} \right. 
\)

%---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

%---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
\newpage
% 2 Objects with General Spin
\subsubsection{2 Objects w/ Any Spin: \ \ \ 
    \(
        \mss{ j_1 \otimes j_2 = (j_1 + j_2) \oplus |j_1 - j_2| }
        \ \Rightarrow\ \mss{ \displaystyle (2j_1+1)(2j_2+1) = \sum_{j=|j_1-j_2|}^{j_1+j_2} 2j+1 } 
    \) 
}

\vspace{5pt} \noindent
\begin{minipage}[t]{.58\textwidth}
    \setlength{\parindent}{.5cm}
    \noindent
    \(\bullet\) \(| \chi_1 \rangle\) has spin, \(j_1\); and \(| \chi_2 \rangle\) has spin, \(j_2\)\\[10pt]
    \(\bullet\) \(j_\text{max} = j_2 + j_1\) and \(j_\text{min} = |j_2 - j_1| \)\\[10pt]
    \(\bullet\) Possible total \(| j \ m \rangle\) must satisfy %
    \begin{center}
        \(\begin{aligned}
            & \boldsymbol{1.)} \ j_\text{min} \leq j \leq j_\text{max},  
                \ \ \ \ \boldsymbol{2.)} \ -j \leq m \leq j, 
                \\[5pt]
            & \boldsymbol{3.)} \ \text{have integer differences}
        \end{aligned}\)
    \end{center}

    \vspace{10pt} If \(j_1\) and \(j_2\) are known from the start,
    \[ \boxed{ 
        \begin{aligned}
            | j \ m \rangle & = \mss{ \sum_{m_1, m_2} 
                | j_{1} \ m_{1} \rangle \otimes | j_{2} \ m_{2} \rangle \
                \langle j_{1} \ m_{1} | \otimes \langle j_{2} \ m_{2} |
                }
                | j \ m \rangle
                \\
            & = \sum_{m_1, m_2} | j_{1} \ m_{1} \rangle \otimes | j_{2} \ m_{2} \rangle \
                C^{j_1 j_2 j}_{m_{1} m_{2} m}
        \end{aligned}
    } \] 
    where the sum is over all poss. int. diff. values that satisfy\\[10pt]
    \(\begin{aligned}
        m_{1} + m_{2} &= m,&  -j_{1} \leq \ &m_{1} \leq j_{1},&   -j_{2} \leq &\ m_{2} \leq j_{2}, 
    \end{aligned}\)\\[10pt]
    and \(C\) are the corresponding Clebsh-Gordan coefficients, whose squared value is
    the probability of measuring the \(\chi_1 \otimes \chi_2\) state represented by that term.
\end{minipage}
\hfill
\fbox{
\begin{minipage}[t]{.33\textwidth}
    \vspace{5pt}
    \begin{center}
        \underline{Possible Combined \( |j \ m\rangle \)}
    \end{center}
    \begin{center} 
        \( \mss{ \begin{aligned}
            (2j_\text{max}+1) & \left\{ \hspace{5pt} \begin{aligned}
                    & \Big| j_\text{max} \ \ j_\text{max} \Big\rangle = \mss{1 \leftarrow\ } \cancel{ e^{i\phi} } \cdot \dots\\
                    & \Big| j_\text{max} \ \ j_\text{max} {\scriptstyle - 1} \Big\rangle \\
                    & \hspace{25pt} \vdots \\
                    & \Big| j_\text{max} \ \ {\scriptstyle -} j_\text{max} \Big\rangle \\
                \end{aligned} \right.
                \\
            (2j_\text{max}-1) & \left\{ \hspace{5pt} \begin{aligned}
                    & \Big| j_\text{max} {\scriptstyle - 1} \ \ j_\text{max} {\scriptstyle - 1} \Big\rangle = 1 \cdot \dots\\
                    & \Big| j_\text{max} {\scriptstyle - 1} \ \ j_\text{max} {\scriptstyle - 2} \Big\rangle \\
                    & \hspace{25pt} \vdots \\
                \end{aligned} \right. 
                \\
            & \hspace{5pt} \vdots
                \\
            (2j_\text{min} + 1) & \left\{ \hspace{5pt} \begin{aligned}
                    & \Big| j_\text{min} \ \ j_\text{min} \Big\rangle = 1 \cdot \dots\\
                    & J_- \Big| j_\text{min} \ \ j_\text{min} \Big\rangle \sim \hs \dots \\
                    & \hspace{25pt} \vdots \\
                    & \Big| j_\text{min} \ \ {\scriptstyle -} j_\text{min} \Big\rangle 
                \end{aligned} \right. 
        \end{aligned} } \) 
    \end{center}
    \vspace{.1cm}
\end{minipage}
}

\vspace{15pt} 
    If the top state in a \(j\)-set (see box above) is known, applying the \(J_-\) lowering operator (and normalizing) %
provides the coefficients for the rest of the set of varying \(m\). %
The coefficients for each top state of a set are (by convention) positive, real, %
and normalized to 1. This makes all of the coefficients real. For the top state of the initial %
\(j_\text{max}\)-set, \( | j_\text{max}\ j_\text{max} \rangle\), %
there is only one product-ket in the sum; its coefficient %
is thus set to 1. For an arbitrary set below the first, the top state has product-ket coefficients such that the state %
is orthogonal to all other previously determined states that have the same \(m\). To reduce some work to solve for them, use %
\[ 
    \begin{aligned}
        C^{j_1 j_2 j}_{m_{1} m_{2} m} & = (-1)^{j_1 + j_2-  j} \cdot C^{j_1 j_2 j}_{-m_{1} -m_{2} -m}\\[5pt]
        \langle j_1 \ m_1 | \langle j_2\ m_2 | j\ m \rangle & 
            = (-1)^{j_1 + j_2-  j} \cdot \langle j_1 \ -m_1 | \langle j_2\ -m_2 | j\ -m\rangle 
    \end{aligned}
\]

\vspace{15pt} 
    If \(m_1\) and \(m_2\) are also known from the start, then \(m = m_1 + m_2\), and
\[ 
    \boxed{ 
        | j_1 \ m_1 \rangle \otimes | j_2 \ m_2 \rangle 
        = \sum_j C^{j_1 j_2 j}_{m_{1} m_{2} m} \ | j \ {\scriptstyle (m_1+m_2)} \rangle 
    } 
\]
where the sum is only over all possible \(s\) as satisfied above - \textbf{1.), 2.) and 3.)}.
In this case, the total z-component, \(m\), is known. The only unknown is the total spin, \(s\), 
whose probability to be measured is \(C^2\).

%
%
%--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
\newpage
\noindent
% Tensor Product Representations
\underline{Tensor Product Representation}\\[10pt]
\(\begin{aligned}
    % Rotation Operators
    \overline{A} \oplus \overline{B} = 
        \mss{ \left[ \begin{matrix}
            A & 0\\
            0 & B
        \end{matrix} \right] }
        ,\ 
        \hsvec{v} \oplus \hsvec{w} = 
        \mss{ \left[ \begin{matrix}
        v\\
        w    
        \end{matrix}\right]}
        & \ \Rightarrow\
        \boxed{ (A \oplus B) (v \oplus w) = Av \oplus Bw }
        \\[5pt]
    A \otimes B = \mss{ \left[ \begin{matrix}
            A_i [B] & A_j [B] \\[2pt]
            A_k [B] & \dots
            \end{matrix} \right] }
        ,\
        v \otimes w = 
        \mss{ \left[ \begin{matrix}
            v_i[w]\\[2pt]
            v_j[w]\\    
        \end{matrix}\right]}
        & \ \Rightarrow\ 
        \boxed{ (A \otimes B) \hs (v \otimes w) = Av \otimes Bw }
        \\[5pt]
    % Generators
    A(t) \otimes B(t) = e^{at} \otimes e^{bt} = e^{ g_{A \otimes B} \hs t } 
        & \ \Rightarrow\
        g_{A \otimes B} = \tfrac{d}{dt} \left( A \otimes B \right) \big|_0 
        = \boxed{ a \otimes \mathbbm{1}_n + \mathbbm{1}_m \otimes b }
        = M_{mn \times mn}
        \\
\end{aligned}\)

\vspace{10pt}\noindent
\(\begin{aligned}
    \text{Lie Algebra}:\ g^{(1,2)} & = g \otimes \mathbbm{1} + \mathbbm{1} \otimes g
        \ \Rightarrow\ 
        \boxed{ g (v \otimes w) = g v \otimes w + v \otimes g w}
        \hspace{15pt}
        ( \mss{ g_z| \nhs \uparrow \uparrow \rangle = 1 | \nhs \uparrow \uparrow \rangle } )
        \\
    \text{Not Lie}:\ (g^2)^{(1,2)} & = (g_+^\dagger)^{(1,2)} (g_+)^{(1,2)} + [g_z^{(1,2)}]^2 + g_z^{(1,2)}\\[5pt]
        & = \boxed{ g^2 \otimes \mathbbm{1} + \mathbbm{1} \otimes g^2 + 2(g_z \otimes g_z) + g_- \otimes g_+ + g_+ \otimes g_- }
\end{aligned}\)

\vspace{10pt}\noindent
\underline{Clebsch-Gordan}:\ \( \mss{
    \Big[ Cl,Go \Big]^T
    \left[ \begin{matrix}
        |\\
        |a\rangle \otimes |b\rangle\\
        |
    \end{matrix} \right]
    = \left[ \begin{matrix}
        |\\
        |i\rangle \oplus |j\rangle\\
        |
    \end{matrix} \right]
    \ \Rightarrow\
    \begin{aligned}
        & \left[ \begin{matrix}
                |\\
                |i\rangle \oplus |j\rangle\\
                |
            \end{matrix} \right]^T
            \\
        \left[ \begin{matrix}
            |\\
            |a\rangle \otimes |b\rangle\\
            |
        \end{matrix} \right]
        & \sqrt{ \Big[ Cl,Go \Big] }
    \end{aligned}
    \hspace{5pt} , \hspace{10pt}
    \begin{aligned}
        & \left[ \begin{matrix}
                1,1 & 1,0 & 0,0 & 1,-1 
            \end{matrix} \right]
            \\
    \left[ \begin{matrix}
            \uparrow \uparrow\\
            \uparrow \downarrow\\
            \downarrow \uparrow\\
            \downarrow \downarrow
        \end{matrix} \right]
        & \sqrt{ \left[ \begin{matrix}
            1 & 0 & 0 & 0\\
            0 & 1/2 & 1/2 & 0\\
            0 & 1/2 & -1/2 & 0\\
            0 & 0 & 0 & 1
        \end{matrix}\right] }
    \end{aligned}
} \)

\vspace{15pt}
